Tickets	Bent Sink 1	Customer Service	care@stylishkb.com	Bent Sink 1	"<div style=""font-size: 13px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Verdana, sans-serif"">
    <div style="""">
        <div style="""">
            <div style="""">
                <div style="""">
                    <div style="""">
                        <div style="""">
                            <div style="""">
                                <div style="""">
                                    <div style="""">
                                        <div style="""">
                                            <div style="""">
                                                <div style="""">
                                                    <div style="""">
                                                        <p><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">Hi,</span></span></p>
                                                        <p><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">We sincerely apologize for the inconvenience you’ve experienced. This situation is quite uncommon and appears to be the result of rough handling by the courier during transit. While the box itself may have arrived undamaged, it’s clear the item sustained some impact.</span></span></p>
                                                        <p><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">Due to the size and weight of our sinks, courier services can sometimes handle packages more roughly than intended. While our packaging includes protective foam and reinforced cardboard, it unfortunately wasn’t enough to fully prevent the bends in this case.</span></span></p>
                                                        <p><strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">The good news:</span></span></strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px""><br>
                                                                    The sink itself remains fully functional for </span></span><em><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">undermount installation</span></span></em><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">. The bends appear limited to the flange, which will not be visible once installed. That said, it’s essential to ensure the sink sits level during installation to prevent water seepage between the countertop and sink.</span></span></p>
                                                        <p><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">Here’s what we recommend:</span></span></p>
                                                        <div>
                                                            <hr><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">
                                                                </span></span>
                                                        </div>
                                                        <h3><strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">Straightening the Flange:</span></span></strong></h3>
                                                        <p><strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">Option 1: Manual Correction</span></span></strong></p>
                                                        <ul>
                                                            <li>
                                                                <div><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">
                                                                        </span></span></div>
                                                                <p><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">Place the sink </span></span><strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">upside down on a soft surface</span></span></strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px""> (e.g., carpet or towel).</span></span></p>
                                                                <div><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">
                                                                        </span></span></div>
                                                            </li>
                                                            <li>
                                                                <div><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">
                                                                        </span></span></div>
                                                                <p><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">Gently tap the bent flange using a </span></span><strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">rubber mallet or hammer</span></span></strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px""> with a protective cloth.</span></span></p>
                                                                <div><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">
                                                                        </span></span></div>
                                                            </li>
                                                            <li>
                                                                <div><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">
                                                                        </span></span></div>
                                                                <p><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">Use a </span></span><strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">level or ruler</span></span></strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px""> to confirm the flange is flat and gaps are under </span></span><strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">1/16""</span></span></strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">, which is sufficient for proper silicone sealing.</span></span></p>
                                                                <div><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">
                                                                        </span></span></div>
                                                            </li>
                                                        </ul>
                                                        <p><strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">Option 2: Pressure Correction During Install</span></span></strong></p>
                                                        <ul>
                                                            <div><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">
                                                                    </span></span></div>
                                                            <li>
                                                                <div><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">
                                                                        </span></span></div>
                                                                <p><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">Use </span></span><strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">clamps and wooden shims</span></span></strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px""> or studs between the flange and countertop during installation to apply pressure and ensure a flush fit.</span></span></p>
                                                                <div><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">
                                                                        </span></span></div>

                                                                                    <font face=""Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">You can pick it up at our warehouse located at:&nbsp;</span></span></font><span style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; letter-spacing: 0.2px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><b style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">85 Thompson Dr, Cambridge, ON N1T 2E4</span></span></b><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">.&nbsp;</span></span></span><span style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif; letter-spacing: 0.2px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">Our business hours are Monday to Friday, 9:00 AM to 5:00 PM.<br style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""></span></span></span>

                                                                                <div style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif; letter-spacing: 0.2px"">
                                                                                        <div style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; letter-spacing: 0.2px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><br style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""></span></span></span></div>
                                                                                        <div style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; letter-spacing: 0.2px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">There is&nbsp;</span></span></span><strong style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; letter-spacing: 0.2px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">no need to call a plumber</span></span></strong><span style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; letter-spacing: 0.2px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">&nbsp;— the hose is very easy to replace on your own. Please follow the updated installation instructions below:<br></span></span></span></div>
                                                                                        <div style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; letter-spacing: 0.2px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><br></span></span></span><span style=""font-size: 13.33px; letter-spacing: 0.2px""><b>How to Replace a Pull-Down Faucet Hose<br></b></span></div>
                                                                                        <div style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; letter-spacing: 0.2px"">
                                                                                                <ol style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">
                                                                                                    <li style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">
                                                                                                        <p style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><strong style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">Turn off the water supply</span></span></strong><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">&nbsp;under the sink.</span></span></p>
                                                                                                    </li>
                                                                                                    <li style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">
                                                                                                        <p style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><strong style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">Disconnect the old hose</span></span></strong><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">&nbsp;from the faucet quickconnector, remove the weight and the spout head.</span></span></p>
                                                                                                    </li>
                                                                                                    <li style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">
                                                                                                        <p style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><strong style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">Pull the old hose out</span></span></strong><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">&nbsp;through the faucet spout.</span></span></p>
                                                                                                    </li>
                                                                                                    <li style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">
                                                                                                        <p style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><strong style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">Feed the new hose through</span></span></strong><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">&nbsp;the spout and down under the sink.</span></span></p>
                                                                                                    </li>
                                                                                                    <li style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">
                                                                                                        <p style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><strong style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">Reconnect the hose</span></span></strong><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">&nbsp;to the faucet quickconnector, reattach the weight and the spout head.</span></span></p>
                                                                                                    </li>
                                                                                                    <li style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">
                                                                                                        <p style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><strong style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">Turn the water back on</span></span></strong><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">&nbsp;and test for proper operation and leaks.</span></span></p>
                                                                                                    </li>
                                                                                                </ol>
                                                                                                <div><strong style=""letter-spacing: 0.2px; box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">Tip:</span></span></strong><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""letter-spacing: 0.2px; box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">&nbsp;Hand-tighten connections, then snug gently if needed—do not overtighten.</span></span></div>
                                                                                                <div><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178size"" style=""letter-spacing: 0.2px; box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; font-size: 13.33px""><span class=""x_1466229844x_919527178font"" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><br></span></span><span style=""font-size: 13.33px; letter-spacing: 0.2px"">If you need any help while installing the handle, feel free to reach out — we’re always happy to assist!<br></span></div>

                                                                    <p style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; letter-spacing: 0.2px""><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">The issue you're experiencing is often caused by mineral buildup or installation debris, and a thorough cleaning usually resolves it. Please follow the steps below to clean your faucet aerator:</span></span></p>
                                                                    <ol style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; letter-spacing: 0.2px"">
                                                                        <li style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">
                                                                            <p style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><strong style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">Remove the spout head</span></span></strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">&nbsp;by unscrewing it from the faucet.</span></span></p>
                                                                        </li>
                                                                        <li style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">
                                                                            <p style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><strong style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">Soak the spout head</span></span></strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">&nbsp;in a 50/50 vinegar and water solution for 24 hours to help dissolve any internal calcification.<br style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">– For faster results, you can use a 50/50 solution of&nbsp;</span></span><strong style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">CLR and water</span></span></strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">&nbsp;and soak the spout head for&nbsp;</span></span><strong style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">10 minutes</span></span></strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">&nbsp;instead.<br style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">– After soaking, gently scrub off any remaining hard water deposits using a toothbrush. We recommend wearing gloves during this process.</span></span></p>
                                                                        </li>
                                                                        <li style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">
                                                                            <p style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><strong style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">If necessary</span></span></strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">, unscrew the aerator from the spout head and clean it separately using the same solution and a toothbrush.</span></span></p>
                                                                        </li>
                                                                        <li style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">
                                                                            <p style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><strong style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">Rinse all parts thoroughly</span></span></strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">, reassemble the components, and test the faucet.</span></span></p>
                                                                        </li>
                                                                    </ol>
                                                                    <p style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; letter-spacing: 0.2px""><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">??&nbsp;</span></span><strong style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">Important:</span></span></strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">&nbsp;Do&nbsp;</span></span><strong style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px""><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">not</span></span></strong><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">&nbsp;fully tighten the aerator, as this can cause the button mechanism to malfunction.</span></span></p>
                                                                    <p style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; letter-spacing: 0.2px""><span class=""font"" style=""font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, sans-serif""><span class=""size"" style=""font-size: 13px"">Once you've completed these steps, please let us know how it goes. We're here to help and will gladly provide further assistance if needed.</span></span></p>
                                                                    <p style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; letter-spacing: 0.2px""></p>
                                                                    <div style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; letter-spacing: 0.2px""><img src=""https://images.thdstatic.com/productImages/3041ab32-0975-4d1d-a6f1-4c763314bd34/svn/clr-calcium-lime-rust-removers-cl-12-64_1000.jpg"" alt=""CLR 28 OZ-Ounce Calcium Lime Rust Remover CL-12 - The Home Depot"" data-zdeskdocid=""img_3508416454981119"" class=""x_642861133docsimage"" data-zdeskdocselectedclass="""" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; letter-spacing: 0.2px; width: 226.008px; height: auto""><img src=""https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcQuBQxbls-vjSWbh9zL8wmmJduETmiS3gVRBQ&amp;s"" data-zdeskdocid=""img_186387473831509"" class=""x_642861133docsimage"" data-zdeskdocselectedclass="""" style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px; max-width: 100%; letter-spacing: 0.2px; width: 218px""></div>

                                                                        <li style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">
                                                                            <p style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">Carefully unscrew the spout head by hand.</p>
                                                                        </li>
                                                                        <li style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">
                                                                            <p style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">Inspect the pulldown hose to see if there is a gasket in place.</p>
                                                                            <ul style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">
                                                                                <li style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">
                                                                                    <p style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">If there is a gasket, please confirm whether it appears to be damaged or in good condition.</p>
                                                                                </li>
                                                                            </ul>
                                                                        </li>
                                                                        <li style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">
                                                                            <p style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">Try re-tightening the spout head to ensure it is securely connected — this may help resolve the issue.</p>
                                                                        </li>
                                                                    </ol>
                                                                    <p style=""box-sizing: border-box; outline: 0px"">Please let us know what you find so we can determine the next best step.</p>

Tickets	Slow water flow	Customer Service	care@stylishkb.com	Slow water flow	"<div style=""font-size: 13px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Verdana, sans-serif"">
    <div>Hi,</div>
    <div><br></div>
    <div>We apologize for the inconvenience. We would like to know if the issue occurred suddenly, or if the flow had been gradually slowing down over time.</div>
    <div>To troubleshoot this issue and determine the cause of the slow water flow, please follow these steps:</div>
    <div><br></div>
    <ol>
        <li style=""list-style-type: decimal"">Remove the spout head (it can be done by hand) and check the water flow. <b>Video Guide</b>: <a href=""https://youtu.be/KZ6dPWnPjwc"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener noreferrer"">https://youtu.be/KZ6dPWnPjwc<br></a></li>
        <li style=""list-style-type: decimal"">Check your water supply shut-off valves—are they fully open? If they are, proceed to step 3.<br></li>
        <li style=""list-style-type: decimal"">Inspect underneath the faucet to ensure none of the hoses are <b>kinked</b>, <b>twisted</b>, or <b>tangled</b>. Check if the pull-out hose moves smoothly. <b>Kinked </b>or <b>twisted </b>hoses can cause a <b>slow flow</b>.<br></li>
        <li style=""list-style-type: decimal"">Verify that the water supply lines from your home plumbing have good water flow and pressure.<br></li>
        <li style=""list-style-type: decimal"">Check whether the slow flow occurs with both hot and cold water, or if it’s specific to one.<br></li>
    </ol>
    <div><br></div>
    <div>If none of the above are causing the issue, the slow flow could be due to a clogged cartridge. Let us know how it goes or if you need further assistance to determine the best course of action.</div>
    <div><br></div>
